## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task models the rate of change of a chemical species concentration (dA_dt) as a function of time and current concentration. The core relationship is a rate law dA/dt = f(A, t), where the functional form depends on the reaction mechanism, order, and whether the system is autonomous or driven.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Zero-order decay: dA_dt = c0 (constant rate, independent of concentration)
- First-order decay: dA_dt = c0 * A (first-order reaction, radioactive decay)
- Second-order decay: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (bimolecular reaction of same species)
- nth-order reaction: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (general power-law rate law)
- Reversible first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 (forward and reverse first-order reactions with equilibrium)
- Mixed order: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2 (competing first and second order pathways)
- Michaelis-Menten type: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A) (enzyme-catalyzed or saturation kinetics)
- Autocatalytic: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (logistic-type autocatalysis)
- Inhibition kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A**2) (substrate inhibition)
- Time-dependent forcing: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (time-dependent source/sink)
- Fractional order with offset: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 + c2 (fractional order with constant production)
- Cooperative kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 / (c2 + A**c1) (Hill-type kinetics)
- Damped oscillatory rate: dA_dt = c0 * A * sin(c1 * t + c2) (periodic forcing on reaction)
- Polynomial rate law: dA_dt = c0 + c1 * A + c2 * A**2 + c3 * A**3 (general polynomial mechanism)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Conservation law constraints → Rate expressions of the form c0 * A * (c1 - A) arise when total concentration is conserved (e.g., A + B = const)
- Enzyme saturation → When rate plateaus at high concentration, Michaelis-Menten form c0 * A / (c1 + A) is appropriate
- Competing parallel reactions → Sum of power-law terms c0 * A**n1 + c1 * A**n2 indicates multiple reaction pathways
- Equilibrium approach → Linear term c0 * A + c1 (with c0 < 0, c1 > 0) indicates relaxation toward equilibrium concentration c1/|c0|
- Cooperativity/sigmoidal response → Hill-type terms A**n / (c + A**n) with n > 1 indicate cooperative binding or multi-step activation
- Stoichiometric coupling → Products of concentration and its complement A*(1-c*A) suggest bimolecular reactions with conservation
- Induction period behavior → Explicit time dependence like (1 - exp(c0*t)) multiplied by rate terms indicates catalyst activation or inhibitor depletion
- Chain reaction mechanisms → Square root dependence A**0.5 arises from steady-state approximation in radical chain reactions

GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t) + c3*_p*sin(c4*A)
Candidate formulas: 50

I need to determine if any candidate formula can be made equivalent to the GT:

**GT:** `-0.1286*sqrt(A) - 0.1286*A*exp(-0.0594*t) + 0.3894*sin(0.5829*A)`

The GT has three terms:
1. A term proportional to `sqrt(A)` = `A^0.5`
2. A term `A*exp(negative*t)`
3. A term `sin(linear_in_A)` (note: no t-dependence in the sin argument)

Let me search for candidates that can produce all three components.

**Candidate 2:** `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4/(c5 + t) + A*c6 + A**c7*c8 + c9`

Setting c0=0, c4=0, the A*c1 and A*c6 merge into A*(c1+c6). Setting c7=0.5 gives `A^0.5 * c8`. The `A*c2*exp(c3*t)` term handles the exponential decay. But we still need `sin(0.5829*A)`. The remaining terms are `A*(c1+c6) + c9`, which are polynomial - can't produce sin. **No match.**

**Candidate 13:** `A*c0/(A**2 + c1) + A*c2 + c3*sin(A*c4 + c5) + c6/(c7*t + c8)`

This has a sin term! `c3*sin(A*c4 + c5)` can match `0.3894*sin(0.5829*A)` with c5=0. But the t-dependence is only `c6/(c7*t + c8)`, which is rational in t, not exponential. The GT needs `A*exp(-0.0594*t)`. **No match.**

**Candidate 31:** `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(c3 + t) + A**c4 + c5*sin(A*c6 + c7) + c8`

Has sin term and `A**c4` (can be sqrt(A)). But t-dependence is `A*c2/(c3+t)`, not exponential. **No match.**

**Candidate 4:** `A**0.5*c0 + A**2*c1 + A*c2 + A*c3/(c4 + t) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t)*log(A*c8 + 1)`

Has `A^0.5`, and `exp(c7*t)*log(A*c8+1)`. The GT needs `A*exp(-ct)` and `sin(cA)`. The `log(A*c8+1)` can't become `A` times something cleanly (unless c8→0 where log(1)=0). And there's no sin. **No match.**

**Candidate 7:** `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4/(c5 + t) + A*c6 + A**c7 + c8`

Has `A*exp(c3*t)` and `A**c7` (set c7=0.5 for sqrt(A)). But no sin term. **No match.**

**Candidate 28:** `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(c3 + t) + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6 + c7/A`

Has `A*exp`, but no sin or sqrt(A). **No match.**

I need a candidate with: (1) `A^0.5` or `A^c`, (2) `A*exp(c*t)`, and (3) `sin(c*A)`.

**Candidate 43:** `A**3*c0 + A**2*c1 + A*c2 + A**c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*t + c7`

Has `A**c3 * exp(c5*t)`. Setting c3=1 gives `A*exp`. But no sin or sqrt(A). **No match.**

Looking more carefully, none of the candidates have both a sin term and an `A*exp(c*t)` term simultaneously, which are both required by the GT.

The only candidates with sin are 13, 16, 31, 37. Let me check 16:

**Candidate 16:** `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(c3 + t) + A**c4 + A**c5*c6*sin(c7*t + c8) + c9`

The sin here depends on t, not A. GT needs sin(cA). **No match.**

**Candidate 37:** `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(c3 + t) + A**c4 + c5*sin(c6*t + c7) + c8` - sin depends on t. **No match.**

None of the candidates can simultaneously produce `sqrt(A)`, `A*exp(-ct)`, and `sin(cA)`.

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t) + c3*_p*sin(c4*A)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.1286*sqrt(A) - 0.1286*A*exp(-0.0594*t) + 0.3894*sin(0.5829*A)`

The GT has three basis functions:
1. `sqrt(A)` — i.e., `A^0.5`
2. `A*exp(-c*t)` — product of A and a decaying exponential in t
3. `sin(c*A)` — sine of A

Let me analyze each candidate for the presence of these basis functions.

**Key observations about GT structure:**
- Contains `sqrt(A)` (A^0.5)
- Contains `A*exp(c*t)` (with c < 0)
- Contains `sin(c*A)` — a trigonometric function of A
- No polynomial terms in A (no A², A³, etc.)
- No terms like `A/(c+t)`, `log(...)`, `1/A`, etc.

For a candidate to match, it must be able to reproduce all three basis functions. Since polynomials, exponentials, sqrt, and sin are linearly independent, the candidate must contain matching basis function types.

Let me check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `A³c0 + A²c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4 + A*c5/(c6+t) + A*c7 + c8 + c9/A`
Has `A*exp(c*t)` ✓, but no `sqrt(A)` or `sin(A)`. Cannot zero out A³, A² etc. while producing sqrt(A) and sin(A). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 2:** `A²c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4/(c5+t) + A*c6 + A^c7*c8 + c9`
Has `A*exp(c*t)` ✓, `A^c7` could be `A^0.5` ✓. But no `sin(A)`. The `A/(c5+t)` term cannot produce sin. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** No exp or sin terms. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 4:** `A^0.5*c0 + A²c1 + A*c2 + A*c3/(c4+t) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t)*log(A*c8+1)`
Has `sqrt(A)` ✓, but `A/(c+t)` ≠ `A*exp(ct)`, and `exp(t)*log(A+1)` ≠ `sin(A)`. No sin, no `A*exp(ct)`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 5:** Rational function in A and t. No sqrt, exp, or sin. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 6:** Has `A*exp(c*t)` but no sqrt(A) or sin(A). **NO MATCH**
